 ) The Union Cabinet on Wednesday decided to ban e-cigarettes completely amid several important decisions
 isko adhyadesh ke zarie lagu karne kii taiyaari he
 This decision has been cited for its increasing addiction among the youth of America, where so far seven deaths have been reported from e-cigarettes
 "cabinet ne i-cigarette par pratibandh lagane kaa faisla kiya he", desh main electronic cigarette par puri tarah pabandi lagane kaa elaan kar vitt mantri nirmala sitaraman ne sabko chaunkaa diya
 It is to be implemented through an ordinance on Wednesday
 is faisale ke tahat na to i cigarette banaai jaaegi, na bechi jaaegi or na hi uskaa prachaar hoga
 For the first time, an e-cigarette businessman can face a year's sentence and a fine of one lakh
 duusari baar pakade jane par 3 saal tak kii sazaa or 5 saal tak kii jail ho sakati he
 Possessing e-cigarettes is also possible with a jail term of 6 months and a fine of up to 50,000
 vitt mantri nirmala sitaraman ne kaha ki "america main saat logon kii maut i-sirget kii vajah se hui he
 Its use there is increasing very fast
 "sarkaar ne america main kii gai research kaa hawala dekar ise sehat ke liye khatarnaak bataaya he
 E-cigarettes were introduced to rid the addiction of common cigarettes
 isamen liquid nicotine hoti he jo garm karne par arosol main badal jaati he
 It is used with battery
 lekin viksit deshon main khaskar yuvaaon or bacchon main ye nai mahamari main badalati dikh rahi he
 The World Health Organization (WHO) also said that electronic cigarettes do the same harm as traditional cigarettes

 We do dusting of most of the household items but often forget the computer keyboard and mouse
 mouse or kii-board aisi chijen hai jinhen saaf karnaa thodaa mushkil hota he
 While cleaning both these things, special care is required
 iejane kis tarah kii-board or mouse kii safai kii ja sakati he

 kii-board kii safai:kii-board ko ulta karke halkaa jhatkein taaki uske kone main fansi dhul va kan baahar gir jaaen
 Then take some cotton and immerse it in alcohol and with the help of it clean the corners of the keyboard
 mouse kii safai:mouse ke pichley hisse main rabar kii coating hoti he jisaki vajah se is par dhul jam jaati he
 Dipping one piece of cotton wool in alcohol will clean the dirt behind the mouse
 uske baad ek or tukdaa rooyee kaa len

 1
 a total of 190 candidates are in the fray for the seven districts of Bastar and 18 assembly seats in Rajnandgaon district of the state, whose fate will be decided by 31,80,014 voters
 2

 3

 4

25 lakh security personnel have been deployed
